============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (PO7)
============================================================
GT: -alpha*v**c0 - beta*Abs(v)**c1 - omega0**c2*x**c3
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed):  
\[
f(x,v)= -1.28311219603499\,x^3\;-\;0.0458938827292319\,v^3\;-\;0.729560991204844\,|v|^{1/3}
\]
No \(t\) dependence, no other powers of \(x\), and the only nonpolynomial term is exactly \(|v|^{1/3}\) (not \(\log\), not \(\sin(\log)\), etc.). A candidate can match if we can set its free constants to reproduce exactly these three terms (possibly under a domain restriction like \(v\ge 0\) to remove \(|\cdot|\) issues).

---

### 1
Has \(x^3\), \(v^3\), plus \(v|v|\) and \(\sin(\log(|v|+1))\). We can zero out unwanted terms, but there is **no way** to turn \(\sin(c\log(c|v|+1)+\phi)\) into \(|v|^{1/3}\) on any continuous domain (they are fundamentally different: bounded/oscillatory vs unbounded power). **No match.**

### 2
Has \(x^3\), \(v^3\), plus \(v|v|\), \(x^5\), and \(\exp(x)\log(|v|+1)\). Can zero unwanted terms, but still cannot create \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No match.**

### 3
Has rational \(v/(c+|v|)\) and \(\exp(x)\log(|v|+1)\); can’t become \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No match.**

### 4
Like (1) but with \(x^5\) instead of \(v^3\). Still no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No match.**

### 5
Includes \(v x^2\) cross-term; can be zeroed, but still only \(\sin(\log)\) available for nonpolynomial \(v\)-dependence, not \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No match.**

### 6
Same issue: only \(\sin(\log(|v|+1))\) for nonpolynomial \(v\). **No match.**

### 7
Has \(t\) via \(\cos(c t)\) and \(\exp(x)\log(|v|+1)\). To match GT (no \(t\)), must set the cosine coefficient to 0. Still no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No match.**

### 8
Has \(1/(c+x)\), \(\exp(x)\log(|c v+c|+1)\), linear \(v\). None can equal \(|v|^{1/3}\) exactly on a continuous domain. **No match.**

### 9
Has \(\sin(\log(|v|+1))\) and polynomial terms; cannot produce \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No match.**

### 10
Has \(t\) cosine and \(\sin(\log)\); cannot produce \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No match.**

### 11
Has \(\sin(c + c\log(c x^2 + c v^2 + 1))\): depends on both \(x\) and \(v\) inside log/sin, cannot reduce to pure \(|v|^{1/3}\) while also keeping the needed \(x^3\) term. **No match.**

### 12
Has \(\exp(\sin(\text{affine in }v))\) plus \(v^3\), etc. Exponential-of-sine cannot equal \(|v|^{1/3}\) on any interval. **No match.**

### 13
Has \(\exp(\sin(\text{affine in }v))\) and \(v|v|\); no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No match.**

### 14
Has \(\exp(\sin(\cdot))\) and \(v\exp(c x)\); no \(|v|^{1/3}\). **No match.**

### 15

GT Equivalence Verification (PO7)
============================================================
GT: -alpha*v**c0 - beta*Abs(v)**c1 - omega0**c2*x**c3
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can exactly match the GT:
$$f(x,v) = -0.0459\,v^3 - 1.283\,x^3 - 0.7296\,|v|^{1/3}$$

The GT has three terms: $v^3$, $x^3$, and $|v|^{1/3}$. Let me check each candidate.

**Key observations about GT:**
- Contains $x^3$ (odd power)
- Contains $v^3$ (odd power)
- Contains $|v|^{1/3}$ (fractional power of absolute value)
- No $x^2$, $x$, constant, $t$-dependent, or other terms

For each candidate, I need to check if the basis functions can reproduce $v^3$, $x^3$, and $|v|^{1/3}$ exactly.

The critical challenge is representing $|v|^{1/3}$. Let me examine which functional forms could potentially represent this.

**Candidate 1:** $c_0 x^3 + c_1 x^2 + c_2 x + c_3 + c_4 v|v| + c_5\sin(c_6\log(c_7|v|+1)+c_8) + c_9 v^3$

Set $c_1=c_2=c_3=0$. Has $x^3$ and $v^3$. But needs $\sin(c_6\log(c_7|v|+1)+c_8)$ to equal $|v|^{1/3}$. The function $\sin(\cdot)$ is bounded between -1 and 1, while $|v|^{1/3}$ is unbounded. Cannot match.

Also, $v|v| = v^2 \text{sgn}(v)$, which is different from $v^3$ (though both are odd). Set $c_4=0$.

Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** $c_0 x^3 + c_1 x + c_2 + c_3 v|v| + c_4 x^5 + c_5 v^3 + c_6\exp(c_7 x)\log(c_8|v|+1)$

Set $c_1=c_2=c_3=c_4=0$. Has $x^3$ and $v^3$. Need $c_6\exp(c_7 x)\log(c_8|v|+1)$ to equal $|v|^{1/3}$. This depends on $x$, so can't match $|v|^{1/3}$ unless $c_7=0$, giving $c_6\log(c_8|v|+1)$. But $\log(c_8|v|+1) \neq |v|^{1/3}$ for all $v$.

Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** Similar issue with $\exp(c_8 x)\log(c_9|v|+1)$ and $v/(c_6+|v|)$.

$v/(c_6+|v|)$ is bounded, can't match $|v|^{1/3}$.

Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** Same sin(log) issue as Candidate 1, bounded. Plus $x^5$ extra.

Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 5:** Same sin(log) bounded issue.

Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 6:** Same sin(log) bounded issue.

Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 7:** $c_0\exp(c_1 x) + c_2 v\cos(c_3 t) + c_4 x + c_5\exp(c_6 x)\log(c_7|v|+1) + c_8 x^3$

Set $c_3=0$: $c_2 v$ term. Set $c_1$ large negative or $c_0=0$. Has $x^3$. Need to produce $v^3$ and $|v|^{1/3}$. $\exp(c_6 x)\log(c_7|v|+1)$ with $c_6=0$ gives $\log(c_7|v|+1)$, not $|v|^{1/3}$. No $v^3$ term available.

Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 8:** No $v^3$ term, $\exp(c_3 x)\log(\cdot)$ can't produce it.

Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 9:** $c_0 x^3 + c_1 x + c_2 + c_3 v|v| + c_4 v + c_5\sin(c_6\log(c_7|v|+1)+c_8)$

sin is bounded, $|v|^{1/3}$ is unbounded.

Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 10-50:** Let me quickly scan for any candidate that has both $v^3$ and $|v|^{1/3}$ (or equivalent).

Looking through all candidates, none have $|v|^{1/3}$ as a basis function. The candidates use $\sin$, $\log$, $\exp$, $v|v|$, $v/(c+|v|)$, etc. None of these can produce $|v|^{1/3}$ exactly.

For candidates 17-18 with Max functions: $\text{Max}(0,v) + \text{Max}(0,-v) = |v|$, not $|v|^{1/3}$.

Candidates 10-50 verdict: [NO MATCH] (all)

[NO MATCH]
